< text>
I've ignored this place for years because it was in a strip mall. So... our favorite pizza place closed and I thought I'd give this place a try. Oh... My... God! Never Will I Ever judge a book by its cover again! The eggplant parmesan was to die for, melt in your mouth, generous portions, absolutely delicious! The fettuccine Alfredo was a miracle in my mouth, and the spaghetti marinara perfect! The Italian salad was generous with plenty of veggies and finally a place that doesn't skimp on the salad dressing they send you! We also ordered the vegetarian pizza and to be honest, it was just ok. It needed more sauce, cheese, and perhaps more herbs in the sauce or somewhere. They were generous with the toppings! We don't eat meat, so I can't vouch for any other pizza, but from the other reviews on a popular food app, people love this place. They have a full menu which gives you plenty of choices. You could eat something different for a month if you came daily. Their prices are good and the service is friendly! This is our new go-to Italian/pizza place!</text>

< Text>
Ordered a pickup of Mango Pomelo/Sago Grass Jelly and Taiwanese popcorn chicken through Grubhub. The order was prompt and ready on arrival.

The Taiwanese popcorn chicken is one of the best I ever had! The soya sauce flavor was right on point, along with the superb batter that complimented the whole thing.

The pudding tasted so good with mango taking the major flavor. The grass jelly was not at all sweet and the only sweetness was from the mango, which again tasted like pure mango. The mango bits were the best part of the whole.

Their menu is really long and I would like to visit the place and try out the rest! This is the best place if you like flavor over sweetness.< /Text>

<Text>Solid cheap bagels. My go to bagel place in the area! Parking is very easy as this place is situated right next to the Safeway.

Owner is very friendly! If you come in a few times, he will recognize you and ask about you which is sweet. The man comes in at 3:30 AM every day to make the bagels. <Text>This is truly a hidden gem. Tucked back in the corner of the shopping center in a non obvious store front, the decor is exactly as you would expect. The service is friendly, sufficient, and not ostentatious. But the food... the food is the star. Inexpensive, supple large portions, and wonderful layers of flavors. Even the standard dishes you can order anywhere, like the szechuan beef, is seriously an all new experience in all the right ways. Fresh crisp vegetables and tender sliced beef with a sauce that comes at you in stages; a little sweet, a little salt and savory, with some earthy tones of garlic and soy. It even finds a way to deliver the "breathe of the wok" characteristic flavor. My family and I have lived in sacramento/Rancho Cordova for more than a decade, and have probably eaten at 80%+ of the available Chinese style restaurants available (past and present), and this by far pleases the mouth more than the others in the area.
A special note should be added regarding the service. The presumed chef/owner is greatly personable, and strives to make sure the food is to your liking. We asked for a special order, not something on the menu. And he did a great job attempting to make it for us. He offered to make another dish for us if his interpretation wasn't correct. That's definitely going above and beyond to accommodate us. Thank you for your efforts!
We really enjoy the food here!< /Text><response>None<//response></record></dataset><record>

<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
This place is a solid breakfast and lunch place for locals and tourists alike. Starting with breakfast, they have a wide selection of coffee and tea drinks. The breakfast sandwiches (design however you please), breakfast rice (amazing to go option and even better as hangover food), and the pastry/mini pie collection all provide ample breakfast options. The lunch selection is mostly sandwich based. The grilled chicken pesto sandwich (pictured) is AMAZEBALLS in the best of ways! Who would have thought a huge grilled red pepper, mustard, and pesto would have made such a good flavor combo, right? This is not a fancy brunch spot, but it is a great place for friends to meet for breakfast or lunch.</Text>

Parking lot is a little strange you enter at the opposite end from the coffee shop and wind around the back to where you saw it from the intersection.< /review>

First time here. Was looking for a simple breakfast. 2 eggs over easy, hash browns and bacon. Instant turn off was you prepay for your breakfast. Then while using the apple payment app it ask if you want to leave a tip. Order it at the counter then pay and get a number. The service was friendly and prompt however the 2 meal $30 breakfast was not. Bacon was very thin and tasted like paper. Hash browns were dry and tasted like old grease. I also ordered a ginger bread cookie and it was very dry and over done around the edges. Not worth the calories. It wasn't worth wasting my time complaining or to reorder. I felt writing this review would be easier. Oh and there was only one bathroom with a long line no toilet paper. I went to Starbucks across the way to order coffee and use the restroom. Other than the friendly staff the experience was disappointing.< /review>

< text>
The pie selection here is pretty extensive. They have pecan, lemon meringue, chocolate silk and way more too. The good thing is the pies are quite small and reasonably priced at around $4.50 each which is perfect for two to share.

The coffee is pretty decent too!

Everything in the cafe is pretty cheap to be honest but is good quality. Is it the best? No, but there is good value for money.

There's no real ambience here so it isn't somewhere you would hang out and it wasn't overly clean when we visited. I'd come back if only for the pies but I wouldn't sit in. It's really close to half moon bay so just grab things to go!< /text>

<Text>On our trip, we made a stop at Half Moon Bay to walk the touristy shops on main street and we ducked into the Half Moon Bay Coffee Company for some lunch.   What a great decision this was.    They have both a great breakfast (which is served all day) and lunch/dinner menu.   A good number of selections available on both.    Here, you stand in line to place your orders, and they give you an order and bring the food to your table.   I choose a patti melt and my husband had a ruebin.   Both were delicious.  Only complaint, if I had to come up with one, is the glass of ice tea was very small and if refills were available, it was not expressed.

They also have a great array of desserts in the case that looked delicious and at reasonable prices for their size (I mean delicious looking concoctions !!!).   But, my jeans are getting tight, so had to pass on them.   The coffee also smelled delicious.
